<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.1।।धृतराष्ट्र ने कहा -- हे संजय ! धर्मभूमि कुरुक्षेत्र में एकत्र हुए युद्ध के इच्छुक (युयुत्सव:) मेरे और पाण्डु के पुत्रों ने क्या किया? [/INST] 1.1 Dhritarashtra said  What did my people and the sons of Pandu do when they had assembled
together eager for battle on the holy plain of Kurukshetra, O Sanjaya. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.2।।संजय ने कहा -- पाण्डव-सैन्य की व्यूह रचना देखकर राजा दुर्योधन ने आचार्य द्रोण के पास जाकर ये वचन कहे। [/INST] 1.2. Sanjaya said  Having seen the army of the Pandavas drawn up in battle-array,
King Duryodhana then approached his teacher (Drona) and spoke these words. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.3।।हे आचार्य ! आपके बुद्धिमान शिष्य द्रुपदपुत्र (धृष्टद्द्युम्न) द्वारा व्यूहाकार खड़ी की गयी पाण्डु पुत्रों की इस महती सेना को देखिये। [/INST] 1.3. "Behold, O Teacher! this mighty army of the sons of Pandu,
arrayed by the son of Drupada, thy wise disciple. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.4।।इस सेना में महान् धनुर्धारी शूर योद्धा है ,  जो युद्ध में भीम और अर्जुन के समान हैं , जैसे --  युयुधान, विराट तथा महारथी राजा द्रुपद। [/INST] 1.4. Here are heroes, mighty archers, eal in battle to Bhima
and Arjuna, Yoyudhana (Satyaki), Virata and Drupada, of the great car (mighty
warriors). </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.5।।धृष्टकेतु, चेकितान, बलवान काशिराज,  पुरुजित्, कुन्तिभोज और मनुष्यों में श्रेष्ठ शैब्य। [/INST] 1.5. "Dhrishtaketu, chekitana and the valiant king of Kasi, Purujit
and Kuntibhoja and Saibya, the best men. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.6।।पराक्रमी युधामन्यु,  बलवान् उत्तमौजा,  सुभद्रापुत्र (अभिमन्यु) और द्रोपदी के पुत्र -- ये सब महारथी हैं। [/INST] 1.6. "The strong Yodhamanyu and the brave Uttamaujas, the son
of Subhadra (Abhimanyu, the son of Subhadra and Arjuna), and the sons of
Draupadi, all of great chariots (great heroes). </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.7।।हे द्विजोत्तम ! हमारे पक्ष में भी जो विशिष्ट योद्धागण हैं , उनको आप जान लीजिये; आपकी जानकारी के लिये अपनी सेना के नायकों के नाम मैं आपको बताता हूँ। [/INST] 1.7. "Know also, O best among the twice-born! the names of those
who are the most distinguished amongst ourselves, the leaders of my army;
these I name to thee for thy information. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.8।।एक तो स्वयं आप, भीष्म, कर्ण, और युद्ध विजयी कृपाचार्य तथा अश्वत्थामा, विकर्ण और सोमदत्त का पुत्र है। [/INST] 1.8. "Thyself and Bhishma, and Karna and also Kripa, the victorious
in war, Asvatthama, Vikarna, and also Bhurisrava, the son of Somadatta. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.9।।मेरे लिए प्राण त्याग करने के लिए तैयार, अनेक प्रकार के शस्त्रास्त्रों से सुसज्जित तथा युद्ध में कुशल और भी अनेक शूर वीर हैं। [/INST] 1.9. "And also many other heroes who are ready to give up their
lives for my sake, armed with various weapons and missiles, all well-skilled
in battle. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.10।।भीष्म के द्वारा हमारी रक्षित सेना अपर्याप्त है; किन्तु भीम द्वारा रक्षित उनकी सेना पर्याप्त है अथवा, भीष्म के द्वारा रक्षित हमारी सेना अपरिमित है किन्तु भीम के द्वारा रक्षित उनकी सेना परिमित ही है। [/INST] 1.10. "This army of ours marshalled by Bhishma is insufficient,
whereas that army of theirs marshelled by Bhima is sufficient. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.11।।विभिन्न मोर्चों पर अपने-अपने स्थान पर स्थित रहते हुए आप सब लोग भीष्म पितामह की ही सब ओर से रक्षा करें। [/INST] 1.11. "Therefore do ye all, stationed in your respective positions,
in the several divisions of the army, protect Bhishma alone." </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.12।।उस समय कौरवों में वृद्ध, प्रतापी पितामह भीष्म ने उस (दुर्योधन) के हृदय में हर्ष उत्पन्न करते हुये उच्च स्वर में गरज कर शंखध्वनि की। [/INST] 1.12. His glorious grandsire (Bhishma), the oldest of the Kauravas,
in order to cheer Duryodhana, now roared like a lion, and blew his conch. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.13।।तत्पश्चात् शंख, नगारे, ढोल व शृंगी आदि वाद्य एक साथ ही बज उठे, जिनका बड़ा भयंकर शब्द हुआ। [/INST] 1.13. Then (following Bhishma), conches and kettledrums, tabors,
drums and cow horns blared forth ite suddenly (from the Kaurava side)
and the sound was tremendous. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.14।।इसके उपरान्त श्वेत अश्वों से युक्त भव्य रथ में बैठे हुये माधव (श्रीकृष्ण) और पाण्डुपुत्र अर्जुन ने भी अपने दिव्य शंख बजाये। [/INST] 1.14. Then, also, Madhava (Krishna) and the son of Pandu (Arjuna),
seated in the magnificent chariot, yoked with white horses, blew divine
conches. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.15।।भगवान् हृषीकेश ने पांचजन्य, धनंजय (अर्जुन) ने देवदत्त तथा भयंकर कर्म करने वाले भीम ने पौण्डू नामक महाशंख बजाया। [/INST] 1.15. Hrishikesha blew the Panchajanya and Arjuna blew the Devadatta
and Bhima (the wolf-bellied), the doer of terrible deeds, blew the great
conch Paundra. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.16।।कुन्तीपुत्र राजा युधिष्ठिर ने अनन्त विजय नामक शंख और नकुल व सहदेव ने क्रमश:  सुघोष और मणिपुष्पक नामक शंख बजाये। [/INST] 1.16. The king Yodhishthira, the son of Kunti, blew the Anantavijaya;
Nakula and Sahadeva blew the Sughosha and the Manipushpaka. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.17।।श्रेष्ठ धनुषवाले काशिराज, महारथी शिखण्डी, धृष्टद्युम्न,  राजा विराट और अजेय सात्यकि। [/INST] 1.17. The king of Kasi, an exellent archer, Sikhandi, the mighty
car-warrior, Dhrishtadyumna and Virata and Satyaki, the unconered. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.18।।हे राजन् ! राजा द्रुपद,  द्रौपदी के पुत्र और महाबाहु सौभद्र (अभिमन्यु) इन सब ने अलग-अलग शंख बजाये। [/INST] 1.18. Drupada and the sons of Draupadi, O Lord of the earth, and
the son of Subhadra, the mighty-armed, blew their conches separately. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.19।।वह भयंकर घोष आकाश और पृथ्वी पर गूँजने लगा और उसने धृतराष्ट्र के पुत्रों के हृदय विदीर्ण कर दिये। [/INST] 1.19. That tumultuous sound rent the hearts of (the members of)
Dhritarashtra's party, making both the heaven and the earth resound. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.20।।हे महीपते ! इस प्रकार जब युद्ध प्रारम्भ होने वाला ही था कि कपिध्वज अर्जुन ने धृतराष्ट्र के पुत्रों को स्थित देखकर धनुष उठाकर भगवान् हृषीकेश से ये शब्द कहे। [/INST] 1.20. Then, seeing the people of Dhritarashtra’s party standing
arrayed and the discharge of weapons about to begin, Arjuna, the son of
Pandu, whose ensign was a monkey, took up his bow and said the following
to Krishna, O Lord of the earth. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.21।।अर्जुन ने कहा -- हे! अच्युत मेरे रथ को दोनों सेनाओं के मध्य खड़ा कीजिये। [/INST] 1.21 Arjuna said  In the middle between the two armies, place my chariot,
O krishna, so that I may behold those who stand here desirous to fight,
and know with whom I must fight, when the battle is about to commence. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.22।।जिससे मैं युद्ध की इच्छा से खड़े इन लोगों का निरीक्षण कर सकूँ कि इस युद्ध में मुझे किनके साथ युद्ध करना है। [/INST] 1.22. Arjuna said  In the middle between the two armies, place my chariot,
O krishna, so that I may behold those who stand here desirous to fight,
and know with whom I must fight, when the battle is about to commence. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.23।।दुर्बुद्धि धार्तराष्ट्र (दुर्योधन) का युद्ध में प्रिय चाहने वाले जो ये राजा लोग यहाँ एकत्र हुए हैं, उन युद्ध करने वालों को मैं देखूँगा। [/INST] 1.23. For I desire to observe those who are assembled here to fight,
wishing to please in battle the evil-minded Duryodhana (the son of Dhritarashtra). </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.24।।संजय ने कहा -- हे भारत (धृतराष्ट्र) ! अर्जुन के इस प्रकार कहने पर भगवान् हृषीकेश ने दोनों सेनाओं के मध्य उत्तम रथ को खड़ा करके। [/INST] 1.24. Sanjaya said  Thus addressed by Arjuna, Krishna, having stationed that
best of chariots, O Dhritarashtra, in the midst of the two armies. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.25।। भीष्म, द्रोण तथा पृथ्वी के समस्त शासकों के समक्ष उन्होंने कहा, "हे पार्थ यहाँ एकत्र हुये कौरवों को देखो"। [/INST] 1.25. In front of Bhishma and Drona, and all the rulers of the
earth, said: "O Arjuna (son of Pritha), behold these Kurus gathered together." </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.26।।वहाँ अर्जुन ने उन दोनों सेनाओं में खड़े पिता के भाइयों,  पितामहों,  आचार्यों,  मामों, भाइयों, पुत्रों,  पौत्रों,  मित्रों,  श्वसुरों और सुहृदों को भी देखा। [/INST] 1.26. Then, Arjuna (son of Pritha) saw there (in the armies) stationed,
fathers and grandfathers, teachers, maternal uncles, brothers, sons, grandsons
and friends too. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.27।।इस प्रकार उन सब बन्धु-बान्धवों को खड़े देखकर कुन्ती पुत्र अर्जुन का मन करुणा से भर गया और विषादयुक्त होकर उसने यह कहा। [/INST] 1.27. (He saw) fathers-in-law and friends also in both the armies.
The son of Kunti, Arjuna, seeing all those kinsmen thus standing arrayed,
spoke this, sorrowfully filled with deep pity. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.28 1.29।।अर्जुन ने कहा -- हे कृष्ण ! युद्ध की इच्छा रखकर उपस्थित हुए इन स्वजनों को देखकर मेरे अंग शिथिल हुये जाते हैं, मुख भी सूख रहा है और मेरे शरीर में कम्प तथा रोमांच हो रहा है।। [/INST] 1.28. Arjuna said  Seeing these, my kinsmen, O krishna, arrayed, eager to fight. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.28 1.29।।अर्जुन ने कहा -- हे कृष्ण !  युद्ध की इच्छा रखकर उपस्थित हुए इन स्वजनों को देखकर मेरे अंग शिथिल हुये जाते हैं,  मुख भी सूख रहा है और मेरे शरीर में कम्प तथा रोमांच हो रहा है। [/INST] 1.29. My limbs fail and my mouth is parched, my body ivers and
my hair stands on end. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.30।।मेरे हाथ से गाण्डीव (धनुष) गिर रहा है और त्वचा जल रही है। मेरा मन भ्रमित सा हो रहा है,  और मैं खड़े रहने में असमर्थ हूँ। [/INST] 1.30. The (bow) Gandiva slips from my hand, and also my skins burns
all over; I am unable even to stand and my mind is reeling, as it were. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.31।।हे केशव ! मैं शकुनों को भी विपरीत ही देख रहा हूँ और युद्ध में (आहवे) अपने स्वजनों को मारकर कोई कल्याण भी नहीं देखता हूँ। [/INST] 1.31. And I see adverse omens, O Kesava. I do not see any good
in killing my kinsmen in battle. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.32।।हे कृष्ण ! मैं न विजय चाहता हूँ, न राज्य और न सुखों को ही चाहता हूँ। हे गोविन्द ! हमें राज्य से अथवा भोगों से और जीने से भी क्या प्रयोजन है?। [/INST] 1.32. I desire not victory, O Krishna, nor kingdom, nor pleasures.
Of what avail is dominion to us, O Krishna, or pleasures or even life? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.33।।हमें जिनके लिये राज्य,  भोग और सुखादि की इच्छा है,  वे ही लोग धन और जीवन की आशा को त्यागकर युद्ध में खड़े हैं। [/INST] 1.33. Those for whose sake we desire kingdom, enjoyments and pleasures,
stand here in battle, having renounced life and wealth. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.34।।वे लोग गुरुजन,  ताऊ,  चाचा,  पुत्र,  पितामह,   श्वसुर,  पोते,  श्यालक तथा अन्य सम्बन्धी हैं। [/INST] 1.34. Teachers, fathers, sons and also grandfathers, maternal uncles,
fathers-in-law, grandsons, brothers-in-law and other relatives,- </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.35।।हे मधुसूदन !  इनके मुझे मारने पर अथवा त्रैलोक्य के राज्य के लिये भी मैं इनको मारना नहीं चाहता,  फिर पृथ्वी के लिए कहना ही क्या है। [/INST] 1.35. These I do not wish to kill, though they kill me, O Krishna,
even for the sake of dominion over the three worlds; leave alone killing
them for the sake of the earth. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.36।।हे जनार्दन ! धृतराष्ट्र के पुत्रों की हत्या करके हमें क्या प्रसन्नता होगी?  इन आततायियों को मारकर तो हमें केवल पाप ही लगेगा। [/INST] 1.36. By killing these sons of Dhritarashtra, what pleasure can
be ours, O Janardana? Only sin will accrue to us from killing these felons. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.37।।हे माधव  !  इसलिये अपने बान्धव धृतराष्ट्र के पुत्रों को मारना हमारे लिए योग्य नहीं है,  क्योंकि स्वजनों को मारकर हम कैसे सुखी होंगे। [/INST] 1.37. Therefore, we should not kill the sons of Dhritarashtra,
our relatives; for how can we be happy by killing our own people, O Madhava
(Krishna)? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.38।।यद्यपि लोभ से भ्रष्टचित्त हुये ये लोग कुलनाशकृत दोष और मित्र द्रोह में पाप नहीं देखते हैं। [/INST] 1.38. Though they, with intelligence overpowered by greed, see
no evil in the destruction of families, and no sin in hostility to friends, </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.39।।परन्तु,  हेे जनार्दन !  कुलक्षय से होने वाले दोष को जानने वाले हम लोगों को इस पाप से विरत होने के लिए क्यों नहीं सोचना चाहिये। [/INST] 1.39. Why should not we who clearly see evil in the destruction
of families, learn to turn away from this sin, O Janardana (Krishna)? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.40।।कुल के नष्ट होने से सनातन धर्म नष्ट हो जाते हैं। धर्म नष्ट होने पर सम्पूर्ण कुल को अधर्म (पाप) दबा लेता है। [/INST] 1.40. In the destruction of a family, the immemorial religious
rites of that family perish; on the destruction of spirituality, impiety,
indeed, overcomes the whole family. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.41।।हे कृष्ण ! पाप के अधिक बढ़ जाने से कुल की स्त्रियां दूषित हो जाती हैं,  और हे वार्ष्णेय ! स्त्रियों के दूषित होने पर वर्णसंकर उत्पन्न होता है। [/INST] 1.41. By the prevalence of impiety, O Krishna, the women of
the family become corrupt; and , women being corrupted, O Varshenya (descendant
of Vrishni), there arises intermingling of castes. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.42।।वह वर्णसंकर कुलघातियों को और कुल को नरक में ले जाने का कारण बनता है। पिण्ड और जलदान की क्रिया से वंचित इनके पितर भी नरक में गिर जाते हैं। [/INST] 1.42. Confusion of castes leads to hell the slayers of the family,
for their forefathers fall, deprived of the offerings of rice-ball and
water (libations). </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.43।।इन वर्णसंकर कारक दोषों से कुलघाती दोषों से सनातन कुलधर्म और जातिधर्म नष्ट हो जाते हैं। [/INST] 1.43. By these evil deeds of the destroyers of the family, which
cause confusion of castes, the eternal religious rites of the caste and
the family are destroyed. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.44।।हे जनार्दन !  हमने सुना है कि जिनके यहां कुल धर्म नष्ट हो जाता है,  उन मनुष्यों का अनियत काल तक नरक में वास होता है। [/INST] 1.44. We have heard, O Janardana, that inevitable is the dwelling
for an unknown period in hell for those men in whose families the religious
practices have been destroyed. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.45।।अहो  !  शोक है कि हम लोग बड़ा भारी पाप करने का निश्चय कर बैठे हैं,  जो कि इस राज्यसुख के लोभ से अपने कुटुम्ब का नाश करने के लिये तैयार हो गये हैं। [/INST] 1.45. Alas! We are involved in a great sin, in that we are
prepared to kill our kinsmen, through greed for the pleasures of a kingdom. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.46।।यदि मुझ शस्त्ररहित और प्रतिकार न करने वाले को ये शस्त्रधारी कौरव रण में मारें,  तो भी वह मेरे लिये कल्याणकारक होगा। [/INST] 1.46. If the sons of Dhritarashtra with weapons in hand should
slay me in battle, unresisting and unarmed, that would be better for me. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।1.47।।संजय ने कहा  --  रणभूमि (संख्ये) में शोक से उद्विग्न मनवाला अर्जुन इस प्रकार कहकर बाणसहित धनुष को त्याग कर रथ के पिछले भाग में बैठ गया। [/INST] 1.47. Sanjaya said  Having thus spoken in the midst of the battlefield, Arjuna,
casting away his bow and arrow, sat down on the seat of the chariot with
his mind overwhelmed with sorrow. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.1।। संजय ने कहा -- इस प्रकार करुणा और विषाद से अभिभूत,  अश्रुपूरित नेत्रों वाले आकुल अर्जुन से मधुसूदन ने यह वाक्य कहा।। [/INST] 2.1 Sanjaya said  To him who was thus overcome with pity and who was despondent, with eyes full of tears and agitated, Madhusudana (the destroyer of Madhu) or Krishna spoke these words. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.2।। श्री भगवान् ने कहा -- हे अर्जुन ! तुमको इस विषम स्थल में यह मोह कहाँ से उत्पन्न हुआ?  यह आर्य आचरण के विपरीत न तो स्वर्ग प्राप्ति का साधन ही है और न कीर्ति कराने वाला ही है।। [/INST] 2.2 The Blessed Lord said  Whence is this perilous strait come upon thee, this dejection which is unworthy of you, disgraceful, and which will close the gates of heaven upon you, O Arjuna? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.3।। हे पार्थ क्लीव (कायर) मत बनो। यह तुम्हारे लिये अशोभनीय है, हे ! परंतप हृदय की क्षुद्र दुर्बलता को त्यागकर खड़े हो जाओ।। [/INST] 2.3 Yield not to impotence, O Arjuna, son of Pritha. It does not befit thee. Cast off this mean weakness of the heart! Stand up, O scorcher of the foes! </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.4।। अर्जुन ने कहा -- हे मधुसूदन ! मैं रणभूमि में किस प्रकार भीष्म और द्रोण के साथ बाणों से युद्ध करूँगा। हे अरिसूदन, वे दोनों ही पूजनीय हैं।। [/INST] 2.4 Arjuna said  How, O Madhusudana, shall I fight in battle with arrows against Bhishma and Drona, who are fit to be worshipped, O destroyer of enemies? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.5।। इन महानुभाव गुरुजनों को मारने से इस लोक में भिक्षा का अन्न भी ग्रहण करना अधिक कल्याण कारक है, क्योंकि गुरुजनों को मारकर मैं इस लोक में रक्तरंजित अर्थ और काम रूप भोगों को ही भोगूँगा।। [/INST] 2.5 Better it is, indeed, in this world to accept alms than to slay the most noble teachers. But if I kill them, even in this world all my enjoyments of wealth and fulfilled desires will be stained with (their) blood. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.6।। हम नहीं जानते कि हमें क्या करना उचित है। हम यह भी नहीं जानते कि हम जीतेंगे, या वे हमको जीतेंगे, जिनको मारकर हम जीवित नहीं रहना चाहते वे ही धृतराष्ट्र के पुत्र हमारे सामने युद्ध के लिए खड़े हैं।। [/INST] 2.6 I can hardly tell which will be better, that we should  coner them or that they should coner us. Even the sons of Dhritarashtra, after slaying whom we do not wish to live, stand facing us. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.7।। करुणा के कलुष से अभिभूत और कर्तव्यपथ पर संभ्रमित हुआ मैं आपसे पूछता हूँ, कि मेरे लिये जो श्रेयष्कर हो, उसे आप निश्चय करके कहिये, क्योंकि मैं आपका शिष्य हूँ; शरण में आये मुझको आप उपदेश दीजिये।। [/INST] 2.7 My heart is overpowered by the taint of pity; my mind is confused as to duty. I ask Thee: Tell me decisively what is good for me. I am Thy disciple. Instruct me who has taken refuge in Thee. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.8।। पृथ्वी पर निष्कण्टक समृद्ध राज्य को और देवताओं के स्वामित्व को प्राप्त होकर भी मैं उस उपाय को नहीं देखता हूँ, जो मेरी इन्द्रियों को सुखाने वाले इस शोक को दूर कर सके।। [/INST] 2.8 I do not see that it would remove this sorrow that burns up my senses, even if I should attain prosperous and unrivalled dominion on earth or lordship over the gods. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.9।। संजय ने कहा -- इस प्रकार गुडाकेश परंतप अर्जुन भगवान् हृषीकेश से यह कहकर कि हे गोविन्द "मैं युद्ध नहीं करूँगा" चुप हो गया।। [/INST] 2.9 Sanjaya said  Having spoken thus to Hrishikesha (the Lord of the senses), Arjuna (the coneror of sleep), the destroyer of foes, said to Krishna, "I will not fight" and became silent. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.10।। हे भारत (धृतराष्ट्र) ! दोनों सेनाओं के बीच में उस शोकमग्न अर्जुन को भगवान् हृषीकेश ने हँसते हुए से यह वचन कहे।। [/INST] 2.10 To him who was despondent in the midst of the two armies, Krishna, as if smiling, O Bharata, spoke these words. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.11।। श्री भगवान् ने कहा -- (अशोच्यान्) जिनके लिये शोक करना उचित नहीं है, उनके लिये तुम शोक करते हो और ज्ञानियों के से वचनों को कहते हो, परन्तु ज्ञानी पुरुष मृत (गतासून्) और जीवित (अगतासून्) दोनों के लिये शोक नहीं करते हैं।। [/INST] 2.11 The Blessed Lord said  Thou hast grieved for those that should not be grieved for, yet thou speakest words of wisdom. The wise grieve neither for the living nor for the dead. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.12।। वास्तव में न तो ऐसा ही है कि मैं किसी काल में नहीं था अथवा तुम नहीं थे अथवा ये राजालोग नहीं थे और न ऐसा ही है कि इससे आगे हम सब नहीं रहेंगे।। [/INST] 2.12 Nor at any time indeed was I not, nor thou, nor these rulers of men, nor verily shall we ever cease to be hereafter. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.13।। जैसे इस देह में देही जीवात्मा की कुमार, युवा और वृद्धावस्था होती है, वैसे ही उसको अन्य शरीर की प्राप्ति होती है;  धीर पुरुष इसमें मोहित नहीं होता है।। [/INST] 2.13 Just as in this body the embodied (soul) passes into childhood, youth and old age, so also does it pass into another body; the firm man does not grieve thereat. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.14।। हे कुन्तीपुत्र ! शीत और उष्ण और सुख दुख को देने वाले इन्द्रिय और विषयों के संयोग का प्रारम्भ और अन्त होता है;  वे अनित्य हैं,  इसलिए,  हे भारत ! उनको तुम सहन करो।। [/INST] 2.14 The contacts of the senses with the objects, O son of Kunti, which cause heat and cold, pleasure and pain, have a beginning and an end; they are impermanent; endure them bravely, O Arjuna. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.15।। हे पुरुषश्रेष्ठ ! दुख और सुख में समान भाव से रहने वाले जिस धीर पुरुष को ये व्यथित नहीं कर सकते हैं वह अमृतत्व (मोक्ष) का अधिकारी होता है।। [/INST] 2.15 That firm man whom, surely, these afflict not, O chief among men, to whom pleasure and pain are the same, is fit for attaining immortality. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.16।। असत् वस्तु का तो अस्तित्व नहीं है और सत् का कभी अभाव नहीं है। इस प्रकार इन दोनों का ही तत्त्व,  तत्त्वदर्शी ज्ञानी पुरुषों के द्वारा देखा गया है।। [/INST] 2.16 The unreal hath no being; there is non-being of the real; the truth about both has been seen by the knowers of the Truth (or the seers of the Essence). </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.17।। उस वस्तु को तुम अविनाशी जानों,  जिससे यह सम्पूर्ण जगत् व्याप्त है। इस अव्यय का नाश करने में कोई भी समर्थ नहीं है।। [/INST] 2.17 Know that to be indestructible, by Which all this is pervaded. None can cause the destruction of That, the Imperishable. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.18।। इस नाशरहित अप्रमेय नित्य देही आत्मा के ये सब शरीर नाशवान् कहे गये हैं। इसलिये हे भारत ! तुम युद्ध करो।। [/INST] 2.18 These bodies of the embodied Self, Which is eternal, indestructible and immeasurable, are said to have an end. Therefore fight, O Arjuna. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.19।। जो इस आत्मा को मारने वाला समझता है और जो इसको मरा समझता है वे दोनों ही नहीं जानते हैं,  क्योंकि यह आत्मा न मरता है और न मारा जाता है।। [/INST] 2.19 He who takes the Self to be the slayer and he who thinks It is slain, neither of them ï1knowsï1. It slays not, nor is It slain. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.20।। यह आत्मा किसी काल में भी न जन्मता है और न मरता है और न यह एक बार होकर फिर अभावरूप होने वाला है। यह आत्मा अजन्मा, नित्य, शाश्वत और पुरातन है,  शरीर के नाश होने पर भी इसका नाश नहीं होता।। [/INST] 2.20 It is not born, nor does It ever die; after having been, It again ceases not to be; unborn, eternal, changeless and ancient, It is not killed when the body is killed. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.21।। हे पार्थ ! जो पुरुष इस आत्मा को अविनाशी,  नित्य और अव्ययस्वरूप जानता है,  वह कैसे किसको मरवायेगा और कैसे किसको मारेगा? [/INST] 2.21 Whosoever knows It to be indestructible, eternal, unborn and inexhaustible, how can that man slay, O Arjuna, or cause to be slain? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.22।। जैसे मनुष्य जीर्ण वस्त्रों को त्यागकर दूसरे नये वस्त्रों को धारण करता है, वैसे ही देही जीवात्मा पुराने शरीरों को त्याग कर दूसरे नए शरीरों को प्राप्त होता है।। [/INST] 2.22 Just as a man casts off worn-out clothes and puts on new ones, so also the embodied Self casts off worn-out bodies and enters others which are new. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.23।। इस आत्मा को शस्त्र काट नहीं सकते और न अग्नि इसे जला सकती है ; जल इसे गीला नहीं कर सकता और वायु इसे सुखा नहीं सकती।। [/INST] 2.23 Weapons cut It not, fire burns It not, water wets It not, wind dries It not. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.24।। क्योंकि यह आत्मा अच्छेद्य (काटी नहीं जा सकती),  अदाह्य (जलाई नहीं जा सकती),  अक्लेद्य (गीली नहीं हो सकती ) और अशोष्य (सुखाई नहीं जा सकती) है;  यह नित्य,  सर्वगत,  स्थाणु (स्थिर),  अचल और सनातन है।। [/INST] 2.24 This Self cannot be cut, burnt, wetted, nor dried up. It is eternal, all-pervading, stable, immovable and ancient. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.25।। यह आत्मा अव्यक्त,  अचिन्त्य और अविकारी कहा जाता है;  इसलिए इसको इस प्रकार जानकर तुमको शोक करना उचित नहीं है।। [/INST] 2.25 This (Self) is said to be unmanifested, unthinkable and unchangeable. Therefore, knowing This to be such, thou shouldst not grieve. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.26।। और यदि तुम आत्मा को नित्य जन्मने और नित्य मरने वाला मानो तो भी,  हे महाबाहो !  इस प्रकार शोक करना तुम्हारे लिए उचित नहीं है।। [/INST] 2.26 But even if thou thinkest of It as being constantly born and constantly dying, even then, O mighty-armed, thou shouldst not grieve. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.27।। जन्मने वाले की मृत्यु निश्चित है और मरने वाले का जन्म निश्चित है;  इसलिए जो अटल है अपरिहार्य - है उसके विषय में तुमको शोक नहीं करना चाहिये।। [/INST] 2.27 For certain is death for the born, and certain is birth for the dead; therefore, over the inevitable thou shouldst not grieve. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.28।। हे भारत ! समस्त प्राणी जन्म से पूर्व और मृत्यु के बाद अव्यक्त अवस्था में रहते हैं और बीच में व्यक्त होते हैं। फिर उसमें चिन्ता या शोक की क्या बात है ? [/INST] 2.28 Beings are unmanifested in their beginning, manifested in their middle state, O Arjuna, and unmanifested again in their end. What is there to grieve about? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.29।। कोई इसे आश्चर्य के समान देखता है;  कोई इसके विषय में आश्चर्य के समान कहता है;  और कोई अन्य पुरुष इसे आश्चर्य के समान सुनता है;  और फिर कोई सुनकर भी नहीं जानता।। [/INST] 2.29 One sees This (the Self) as a wonder; another speaks of It as a wonder; another hears of It as a wonder; yet having heard, none understands It at all. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.30।। हे भारत ! यह देही आत्मा सबके शरीर में सदा ही अवध्य है, इसलिए समस्त प्राणियों के लिए तुम्हें शोक करना उचित नहीं।। [/INST] 2.30 This, the Indweller in the body of everyone, is ever indestructible, O Arjuna; therefore, thou shouldst not grieve for any creature. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.31।। और स्वधर्म को भी देखकर तुमको विचलित होना उचित नहीं है,  क्योंकि धर्मयुक्त युद्ध से बढ़कर दूसरा कोई कल्याणकारक कर्त्तव्य क्षत्रिय के लिये नहीं है।। [/INST] 2.31 Further, having regard to thy duty, shouldst not waver, for there is nothing higher for a Kshatriya than a righteous war. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.32।। और हे पार्थ ! अपने आप प्राप्त हुए और स्वर्ग के लिए खुले हुए द्वाररूप इस प्रकार के युद्ध को भाग्यवान क्षत्रिय लोग ही पाते हैं।। [/INST] 2.32 Happy are the Kshatriyas, O Arjuna! who are called upon to fight in such a battle that comes of itself as an open door to heaven. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.33।। और यदि तुम इस धर्मयुद्ध को स्वीकार नहीं करोगे,  तो स्वधर्म और कीर्ति को खोकर पाप को प्राप्त करोगे।। [/INST] 2.33 But if thou wilt not fight this righteous war, then having abandoned thine own duty and fame, thou shalt incur sin. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.34।। और सब लोग तुम्हारी बहुत काल तक रहने वाली अपकीर्ति को भी कहते रहेंगे;  और सम्मानित पुरुष के लिए अपकीर्ति मरण से भी अधिक होती है।। [/INST] 2.34 People, too, will recount thy everlasting dishonour; and to one who has been honoured, dishonour is worse than death. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.35।। और जिनके लिए तुम बहुत माननीय हो उनके लिए अब तुम तुच्छता को प्राप्त होओगे,  वे महारथी लोग तुम्हें भय के कारण युद्ध से निवृत्त हुआ मानेंगे।। [/INST] 2.35 The great car-warriors will think that thou hast withdrawn from the battle through fear; and thou wilt be lightly held by them who have thought much of thee. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.36।। तुम्हारे शत्रु तुम्हारे सार्मथ्य की निन्दा करते हुए बहुत से अकथनीय वचनों को कहेंगे,  फिर उससे अधिक दु:ख क्या होगा ? [/INST] 2.36 Thy enemies also, cavilling at thy power, will speak many abusive words. What is more painful than this? </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.37।। युद्ध में मरकर तुम स्वर्ग प्राप्त करोगे या जीतकर पृथ्वी को भोगोगे;  इसलिय, हे कौन्तेय ! युद्ध का निश्चय कर तुम खड़े हो जाओ।। [/INST] 2.37 Slain, thou wilt obtain heaven; victorious, thou wilt enjoy the earth; therefore, stand up, O son of Kunti, resolved to fight. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.38।। सुख-दु:ख,  लाभ-हानि और जय-पराजय को समान करके युद्ध के लिये तैयार हो जाओ;  इस प्रकार तुमको पाप नहीं होगा।। [/INST] 2.38 Having made pleasure and pain, gain and loss, victory and defeat the same, engage thou in battle for the sake of battle; thus thou shalt not incur sin. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.39।। हे पार्थ ! तुम्हें सांख्य विषयक ज्ञान कहा गया और अब इस (कर्म) योग से सम्बन्धित ज्ञान को सुनो जिस ज्ञान से युक्त होकर तुम कर्मबन्ध का नाश कर सकोगे।। [/INST] 2.39 This, which has been taught to thee, is wisdon concerning Sankhya. Now listen to wisdom concerning Yoga, endowed with which, O Arjuna, thou shalt cast off the bonds of action. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.40।। इसमें क्रमनाश और प्रत्यवाय दोष नहीं है। इस धर्म (योग) का अल्प अभ्यास भी महान् भय से रक्षण करता है।। [/INST] 2.40 In this there is no loss of effort, nor is there any harm (production of contrary results or transgression). Even a little of this knowledge (even a little practice of this Yoga) protects one from great fear. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.41।। हे कुरुनन्दन ! इस (विषय) में निश्चयात्मक बुद्धि एक ही है, अज्ञानी पुरुषों की बुद्धियां (संकल्प) बहुत भेदों वाली और अनन्त होती हैं।। [/INST] 2.41 Here, O joy of the Kurus, there is but a single one-pointed determination; many-branched and endless are the thoughts of the irresolute. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.42।। हे पार्थ  अविवेकी पुरुष वेदवाद में रमते हुये जो यह पुष्पिता (दिखावटी शोभा की) वाणी बोलते हैं? इससे (स्वर्ग से) बढ़कर और कुछ नहीं है।।। [/INST] 2.42 Flowery speech is uttered by the unwise, taking pleasure in the eulogising words of the Vedas, O Arjuna, saying, "There is nothing else." </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.43।। कामनाओं से युक्त? स्वर्ग को ही श्रेष्ठ मानने वाले लोग भोग और ऐश्वर्य को प्राप्त कराने वाली अनेक क्रियाओं को बताते हैं जो (वास्तव में) जन्मरूप कर्मफल को देने वाली होती हैं।। [/INST] 2.43 Full of desires, having heaven as their goal, (they utter speech which is directed to ends) leading to new births as the result of their works, and prescribe various methods abounding in specific actions, for the attainment of pleasure and power. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.44।।उससे जिनका चित्त हर लिया गया है ऐसे भोग और एश्र्वर्य‌ मॆ आसक्ति रखने वाले पुरुषों के अन्तकरण मे निश्चयात्मक् बुद्धि नही हॊती अर्थात वे ध्यान का अभ्यास करने योग्य‌ नही होते। [/INST] 2.44 For those who are attached to pleasure and power, whose minds are drawn away by such teaching, ï1thatï1 determinate reason is not formed which is steadily bent on meditation and Samadhi (superconscious state). </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.45।। हे अर्जुन  वेदों का विषय तीन गुणों से सम्बन्धित (संसार से) है  तुम त्रिगुणातीत? निर्द्वन्द्व? नित्य सत्त्व (शुद्धता) में स्थित? योगक्षेम से रहित और आत्मवान् बनो।। [/INST] 2.45 The Vedas deal with the three attributes (of Nature); be thou above these three attributes. <s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.46।। सब ओर से परिपूर्ण जलराशि के होने पर मनुष्य का छोटे जलाशय में जितना प्रयोजन रहता है? आत्मज्ञानी ब्राह्मण का सभी वेदों में उतना ही प्रयोजन रहता है।। [/INST] 2.46 To the Brahmana who has known the Self, all the Vedas are of as much use as is a reservoir of water in a place where there is a flood. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.47।। कर्म करने मात्र में तुम्हारा अधिकार है? फल में कभी नहीं। तुम कर्मफल के हेतु वाले मत होना और अकर्म में भी तुम्हारी आसक्ति न हो।। [/INST] 2.47 Thy right is to work only, but never with its fruits; let not the fruits of action be thy motive, nor let thy attachment be to inaction. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.48।। हे धनंजय  आसक्ति को त्याग कर तथा सिद्धि और असिद्धि में समभाव होकर योग में स्थित हुये तुम कर्म करो। यह समभाव ही योग कहलाता है।। [/INST] 2.48 Perform action, O Arjuna, being steadfast in Yoga, abandoning attachment and balanced in success and failure. <s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.49।। इस बुद्धियोग की तुलना में(सकाम) कर्म अत्यन्त निकृष्ट हैं? इसलिये हे धनंजय  तुम बद्धि की शरण लो फल की इच्छा करनेवाले कृपण (दीन) हैं।। [/INST] 2.49 Far lower than the Yoga of wisdon is action, O Arjuna. <s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.50।। समत्वबुद्धि युक्त पुरुष यहां (इस जीवन में) पुण्य और पाप इन दोनों कर्मों को त्याग देता है? इसलिये तुम योग से युक्त हो जाओ। कर्मों में कुशलता योग है।। [/INST] 2.50 Endowed with wisdom (evenness of mind), one casts off in this life both good and evil deeds; therefore, devote thyself to Yoga; Yoga is skill in action. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.51।। बुद्धियोग युक्त मनीषी लोग कर्मजन्य फलों को त्यागकर जन्मरूप बन्धन से मुक्त हुये अनामय अर्थात् निर्दोष पद को प्राप्त होते हैं।। [/INST] 2.51 The wise, possessed of knowledge, having abandoned the fruits of their actions, and being freed from the fetters of birth, go to the place which is beyond all evil. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.52।। जब तुम्हारी बुद्धि मोहरूप दलदल (कलिल) को तर जायेगी तब तुम उन सब वस्तुओं से निर्वेद (वैराग्य) को प्राप्त हो जाओगे? जो सुनने योग्य और सुनी हुई हैं।। [/INST] 2.52 When thy intellect crosses beyond the mire of delusion, then thou shalt attain to indifference as to what has been heard and what has yet to be heard. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.53।। जब अनेक प्रकार के विषयों को सुनने से विचलित हुई तुम्हारी बुद्धि आत्मस्वरूप में अचल और स्थिर हो जायेगी तब तुम (परमार्थ) योग को प्राप्त करोगे।। [/INST] 2.53 When thy intellect, which is perplexed by the Veda text, which thou hast read, shall stand immovable and steady in the Self, then thou shalt attain Self-realisation. </s>
<s>[INST] What is English commentary of this Hindi Shloka in Bhagvath Gita:  ।।2.54।। अर्जुन ने कहा -- हे केशव  समाधि में स्थित स्थिर बुद्धि वाले पुरुष का क्या लक्षण है स्थिर बुद्धि पुरुष कैसे बोलता है कैसे बैठता है  कैसे चलता है [/INST] 2.54 Arjuna said  What, O Krishna, is the description of him who has steady wisdom, and is merged in the superconscious state?
